 haq kii khatir gwalior se dilli tak kii padayatra par nikle jansatyagraiyon kaa kafila uttar pradesh ke agra main he
 Madhya Pradesh Chief Minister Shivraj Singh Chauhan, who reached out to support these satyagrahis, has assured that he will first implement the land reform policy approved by the central government in his state
 udhar ummid jataai ja rahi he ki 11 oktober ko kendriya gramin vikaas mantri jairam ramesh kii maujuudagi main agra main samjhaute par hastakshar hoga
 It is to be known that the Jansatyagraha 2012 started from Gwalior on 2 October under the leadership of the Chairman of Ekta Parishad, PV Rajagopal, for the demand of giving land to the landless, including the overall policy of land reform
 in satyagraiyon ko manaane kii centre sarkaar kii ore se koshishen jari hai, vahiin satyagrahi likhit samjhaute se kam par maanane ko taiyaar nahin hai
 To support these Satyagrahis, Madhya Pradesh Chief Minister Shivraj Singh Chauhan arrived in Agra on Thursday along with his wife Sadhna Singh and Women Child Development Minister Ranjana Baghel and also participated in the padyatra with him
 is maukey par mukhyamantri ne kaha ki mapra main garib bhoomihin jahaan kabiz hai unhen us jagah kaa patta de diya jayega chaahe vah sarkari jagah ho yaa gaiyr sarkari
 He has asked the Central Government to bring the National Land Reform Policy at the earliest, saying that the state government will also implement it fully
 mukhyamantri agra ke paas rohta main padayatra main shaamil hue or patni sadhana singh ke saath khuli jeep main lagbhag paanch kimi tak bhoomihin, vanchit va adivaasiyon ke bich chale
 Chauhan told reporters that his state government will withdraw all the cases against the tribals, except for the serious matters
 tippaniyan It is noteworthy that talks have been held between the representatives of the agitators and Union Rural Development Minister Jairam Ramesh on Monday and again in Delhi on the demands of public satyagrahis and some issues have been agreed
